PROJECT WARRIORS - CONSOLIDATED MASTER SOURCE FILE

Purpose: Single plain-text source file consolidating the uploaded source materials into one human-readable and AI-reference-friendly document.

Consolidation rules used:
- Included all uploaded text sources.
- Included the PDF as extracted text using pdftotext, with page breaks marked as [PDF PAGE BREAK].
- Excluded raw image binary, but preserved the uploaded PNG as a text description appendix.
- Preserved original filenames for cross-reference.
- When two files were byte-identical, both were listed in the manifest, but the duplicate file was not reprinted verbatim.

NAVIGATION TIPS:
- Search for DOC-### to jump to a specific source.
- Search for "Original filename:" to find the exact source file name.
- Search for section headers such as SECTION 02 - CHARACTERS or SECTION 04 - WEAPONS.

PROJECT WARRIORS — META THREAD DEVELOPMENT SUMMARY
For upload to Project Knowledge
Last updated: April 2026
Status markers: [LOCKED] = confirmed and final | [DEVELOPMENT] = in progress | [CONCEPT] = early stage, needs work | [PINNED] = noted for future development in appropriate thread
========================================================


SECTION 1 — PROJECT IDENTITY & NAMING
========================================================

STUDIO NAME [LOCKED]
Tears in the Rain (TITR)
Reference: Roy Batty's monologue, Blade Runner (1982). Rationale: the game gives the player a chance to witness things they'd never believe — the scale and weight of a world at war glimpsed through the eyes of individuals caught inside it. The studio name reflects this thematic core.

STUDIO LOGO [DEVELOPMENT]
- Four letters: T I T R, centered
- T and R slightly larger than I and the second T (grammatical words carry less visual weight)
- Angular / trapezoidal composition — cassette futurism aesthetic inspired by Weyland-Yutani (Alien) and Tyrell Corporation (Blade Runner) logo design language
- To be displayed on a CRT-style screen in the studio splash sequence (see below)
- Design direction confirmed; final visual execution TBD

STUDIO DESCRIPTOR [LOCKED]
"Virtual Entertainment Software"
— displayed beneath the TITR logo on the splash screen

STUDIO SPLASH SEQUENCE [DEVELOPMENT]
- Duration: 5–6 seconds maximum
- Camera: slightly off-axis from screen — not fully head-on. Physical environment visible around the device (bezel, chassis, ambient surroundings)
- Screen aesthetic: CRT phosphor, green or green-and-white palette, scanlines, slight curvature
- Loading bars or test pattern before logo resolves — suggests data loading from tape or slow media source
- Device brand badge: SOLITON TYPE-1 — reference to Soliton Radar System from Metal Gear Solid (1998); "Soliton" is also a real physics term so trademark risk is low; TYPE-1 is a clean period-appropriate model designation
- Environmental Easter eggs visible in peripheral frame (all subtle, never foregrounded):
  * Pack of Moslems cigarettes (Snake's brand, MGS1) — partially cut off at frame edge
  * Hope County sticker (Far Cry 5) — on the side of the device or a nearby mug
  * Montrose, Colorado postcard (Homefront) — partially visible at frame edge
  NOTE: Do not use all three simultaneously — pick two maximum to avoid crowding. Moslems + Hope County sticker is the recommended combination.
- Full visual design execution TBD — flagged for dedicated design session


PROJECT / GAME WORKING TITLE [LOCKED]
Project Warriors

TRILOGY INSTALMENT TITLES [LOCKED]
- Project Warriors I
- Project Warriors II
- Project Warriors III
- Project Warriors: Sea Spear (Nereid Black DLC)


========================================================


SECTION 2 — GAME STRUCTURE & PLAYABLE CHARACTERS
========================================================

MAIN TRILOGY — PLAYABLE CHARACTERS [LOCKED]
- Romeo (LT Ramón Álvarez) — playable across Games 1, 2, 3
- Ducky (SFC Ferris Ryan) — playable across Games 1, 2, 3
- Spook (CPT Trevor Gartner) — playable across Games 1, 2, 3
- Frost (Aki Peltola) — playable in Cold Frontier flashback only
- Additional story-adjacent characters may be playable in one-off flashback or significant narrative sequences — TBD

SEA SPEAR DLC — PLAYABLE CHARACTER [LOCKED]
- Grim — sole playable character
- Rest of Nereid Black (Rime, Undertow, Lantern) are NPC squadmates
- Potential for switching between Nereid Black members discussed but shelved — may revisit to add contrast later

GAME 2 — CAMPAIGN ARCHITECTURE [LOCKED]
Three campaigns:
1. Romeo — American Freedom ("War Hits Home")
2. Ducky — Persistent Threat ("The System Fell. We Didn't.")
3. Spook — Godkiller ("You Can't Kill a Dead Man")


========================================================


SECTION 3 — DLC LINEUP
========================================================

PROJECT WARRIORS: SEA SPEAR [DEVELOPMENT]
- Nereid Black campaign
- Grim sole playable character
- Standalone storyline — not a mission pack
- Approx. 60% length of a main instalment (provisional)
- Position in overall story timeline TBD
- Story not yet developed

PROJECT WARRIORS: SEMPER FI [CONCEPT]
- US Marines, West Coast campaign
- Protagonist: Staff Sergeant Andre Nathaniel Bridges
- Timeframe: approx. 30 days post-PANDORA, overlapping with period before and during Game 1 and potentially Game 2 Romeo campaigns
- Locations: Seattle and other West Coast sites
- Narrative focus: immediate military response to PANDORA in severely degraded operational conditions — Marines fighting without usual technological and logistical support
- Seeded through Romeo's Signal Hill and Coronado missions in Game 1
- Overlap with main campaign timelines TBD
- Story not yet developed beyond concept

PROJECT WARRIORS: WHO DARES WINS [CONCEPT]
- SAS campaign
- Title confirmed — "Who Dares Wins" is the actual SAS motto
- Protagonist TBD
- Covers SAS deployment operations AND the British home front — how Britain responded to PANDORA and the subsequent war
- Possible overlap with Game 3 Boston campaign
- Possible SBS / Nereid Black crossover
- Story not yet developed

PROJECT WARRIORS: HOME DEFENSE [CONCEPT]
- Australian front, China Pacific arc
- Protagonist TBD — Australian armed forces, branch TBD
- Tied to Game 3 — China's northeastern Australian coastal invasion
- Switchblade (Australian) may have a connection to this DLC protagonist
- Title provisional — likely to change as story develops
- Story not yet developed

NOTE ON MIDDLE EASTERN THEATER: China moves into the Middle East in Game 3 to secure mineral reserves and strategic positions. A Middle Eastern theater campaign arc is planned — may be a Game 3 campaign segment or a separate DLC. Not yet determined. Pinned for Game 3 development.


========================================================


SECTION 4 — CAMPAIGN & MISSION STAMPS (UI VISUAL DESIGN)
========================================================

STATUS: [DEVELOPMENT] — concept confirmed, visual execution TBD

Each campaign has a distinct visual style for the mission timestamp / location card displayed at the start of each mission. Standard information displayed: local time (military format), date, location, operation name, character/team designation.

SPOOK [CONFIRMED CONCEPT]
Typewriter font. Information appears then gets redacted — specific words crossed out with black tape before the card fades out. Thematically perfect for a CIA operative whose entire story is about things being hidden. The information appears, the player reads it, and then it gets classified right in front of them.

DUCKY [CONFIRMED CONCEPT]
Green phosphor / digital tactical display font — similar to DAOG command interface aesthetic. Subtle scanline effect or faint grid overlay suggested. Clean, functional, military.

ROMEO [CONCEPT — NOT YET DECIDED]
Options under consideration:
- Stencil font (military equipment / crate aesthetic)
- Handwritten on a map or resistance planning board (fits AFC guerrilla aesthetic, especially Game 2)
- Worn paper / field document (physical order or briefing sheet, slightly crumpled)
Handwritten-on-map is the current preference — completely distinct from Spook's typewriter and Ducky's tactical display, anchors Romeo in the physical improvised world of his campaigns.
DECISION PENDING.


========================================================


SECTION 5 — CHARACTER UPDATES & ADDITIONS
========================================================

LT. TARA HALLIDAY — CALLSIGN ADDED [LOCKED]
Callsign: ORACLE
Rationale: fits the Greek mythology naming convention of DAOG command structure (ZEUS, ARES, PYTHIA etc.); thematically appropriate for Senior Operations Intelligence Analyst — the oracle sees what others don't. Confirmed alongside PYTHIA (counterintelligence unit) without conflict.

NAVARRE & BUDANOVA — NEW IDENTITIES [LOCKED]
Following player choice to help them escape in Game 1:
- Simenon Christophe Navarre → Simon-Pierre Aubert, Swiss French identity, semi-retired freight consultant, Évora, Alentejo, Portugal
- Karyna Budanova → Katja Reimann, Austrian identity, same location

RELOCATION: Évora, Alentejo, Portugal [LOCKED]
- UNESCO World Heritage city, small but active expat community, affordable, quiet, predominantly Portuguese demographic
- Navarre's character detail: alt-right media diet shaped by benzos-softened conspiratorial thinking; still watching the same content in Évora that he watched in Frankfurt — half-drawn curtains, large screen, audio bleed suggesting Jones/Rogan cadence (never named, never shown clearly)
- Budanova does the actual living — buys groceries, learns Portuguese, makes limited contact with neighbours
- Navarre's farewell call to Spook in Game 2 comes from Évora

DUCKY — BOSTON ORIGIN [LOCKED]
Ducky is from Boston. He hasn't lived there for a long time. This is revealed through environmental storytelling, not dialogue:
- A photo of a modest upper-middle-class Boston suburb house appears in Ducky's quarters at Insworth (accessible in free roam at start of Game 1 campaign) — on a desk, slightly angled away, only fully visible if the player walks to the end of the room and turns around
- The same house appears in the Boston suburb mission in Romeo's Game 3 campaign — the player as Romeo can find it if attentive; never explicitly identified as Ducky's childhood home
- House details (to be developed in narrative thread):
  * Parents alive — fled or evacuated before/during occupation; intend to return
  * Back of house: carport with a vintage Dodge Charger mid-restoration, hood up, tools laid out, hobby project state
  * On a workbench/parts catalogue: handwritten note clipped to manual page — "Edelbrock Supercharged GEN III 426 HEMI Crate Engine, part number #46126 / Backorder placed / ETA in stock 3/2029"
  * Kitchen: travel planning list pinned to fridge or board — a high-stakes holiday that was being prepared before the occupation; the trip date has already passed; nobody cancelled it
  * Inside: Ducky's childhood room — sports pennants, high school photos, possible Irish heritage references (GAA jersey, flag, parish photo), possible family military history reference
- Continuity: the state of the Boston neighborhood (Russian occupied vs. contested vs. cleared) TBD pending Boston campaign development — will affect mission design and house accessibility

LUPIN — AGE AND BACKSTORY [DEVELOPMENT — moved to character thread]
- Born 1992, Reşiţa, Caraș-Severin County, Romania
- Full backstory developed in Meta thread, now relocated to character backstory thread
- Key notes: post-revolutionary Romania context; father a laid-off steelworker; mother a schoolteacher who lived under the Securitate; quiet resilience as emotional core; Romanian SOF career pathway through NATO integration era; callsign origin (Arsène Lupin or lupin flowers in poor soil) — TBD
- Age at time of games (2028): 35–36


========================================================


SECTION 6 — THEMATIC & NARRATIVE FLAVOR
========================================================

GAME CONCEPT BLURB [LOCKED — draft, subject to refinement]
"This is a tactical shooter. It aspires to be a good one — and hopefully succeeds. It will recommend realism. But for the players who follow the story, the game isn't really about the shooting.

It's about people. Extraordinary people, mostly — but still human. They're capable. They know how to fight. They are warriors.

This is a story of people who are good at surviving, caught in a war that each of them, in their own way, chose to fight. A war they didn't start. A war they most likely cannot end. They can only hope to make the right choices, to do their best, and to live to fight another day."

NOTE: "Warriors" is deliberately chosen to encompass both military and civilian protagonists — the game's cast includes non-military characters (Ebonn, resistance cell members, civilians caught in the war) as well as operators.

THE NORTH STAR [LOCKED — internal creative reference]
The goal for trailers and promotional material: the player sees it on their screen and thinks "holy shit, when is this out?" This feeling — generated by the Good Morning America teaser, by the aircraft scenes, by the paratroopers over the Smoky Mountains — is the benchmark.


========================================================


SECTION 7 — EASTER EGGS & REFERENCES (confirmed)
========================================================

ATLAS RECRUITMENT POSTER — "FEEL LIKE A HERO" [LOCKED]
- Poster text: "Feel like a hero" — slightly off, slightly hollow, satirical PMC recruitment aesthetic
- Appears: seeded across Game 1 in Atlas and GenCorp-adjacent environments (Romeo sees it in LA, Ducky encounters it in European GenCorp/Atlas locations, Spook sees it in Frankfurt)
- Payoff: In Abu Dhabi (Spook, Game 1, mission: Infrastructure Day) — in a bathroom, the poster has been vandalized in red marker. The modified text reads: "Do you feel like a hero yet?"
- Reference: Spec Ops: The Line (2012) — Colonel Konrad's iconic line. Never stated or acknowledged in game.
- The poster can reappear as a background asset in Games 2 and 3 as a callback, but the arc (setup and payoff) is entirely within Game 1.
- Status: LOCKED

SPEC OPS: THE LINE — "GENTLEMEN, WELCOME TO ABU DHABI" [LOCKED]
- Spook delivers this line upon arrival in Abu Dhabi (Infrastructure Day mission) — mirror of Captain Walker's "Gentlemen, welcome to Dubai" from Spec Ops: The Line
- Delivered by Spook (not Smoke) — mirrors Walker as mission lead
- Timing: helicopter approach or landing
- Status: LOCKED

METAL GEAR SOLID — SOLITON DEVICE BADGE [LOCKED]
- On the device in the studio splash sequence: small badge reading "SOLITON TYPE-1"
- Soliton Radar is an iconic MGS1 item; "Soliton" is also a real physics term (self-reinforcing wave) so trademark risk is low
- TYPE-1 is the model designation — clean, period appropriate, avoids direct MGS abbreviation
- Status: LOCKED

RED DAWN (1984) — PARATROOPER DROP [LOCKED]
- See Scene 4 in aircraft scenes document
- Status: LOCKED — execution TBD

LEAVE THE WORLD BEHIND — PANDORA ATTACK CINEMATIC [PINNED]
- A short cinematic sequence depicting the immediate aftermath of PANDORA attacks from the POV of anonymous temporary playable characters (civilians)
- One proposed scene: hikers in upstate New York (area similar to the film's setting) emerge from treeline to see a river/body of water with a city skyline beyond it — smoke columns rising, autonomous drones swarming, sporadic fires. The horror arrives obliquely through nature and ordinary life.
- Serves to establish the scale and shock of the attacks from a civilian ground-level perspective
- To be developed — narrative thread

SECTION 8 — MUSIC (AEGIS SQUAD PROMO CLIPS)
========================================================

FORMAT [LOCKED]
Solo character profile promo videos. Dynamic fast-cut action footage set to a character-defining song. Two versions each: 90-second cut (trailers/social) and full track length (deeper engagement pre-release). Tone varies by character. Starting with AEGIS Squad.

CONFIRMED TRACKS [LOCKED]
- Switchblade — Fight Like a Girl, Evanescence ft. K.Flay
- Frost — Helvegen, Wardruna
- Ducky — I'm Shipping Up to Boston, Dropkick Murphys
  NOTE: This song may also be reserved for a narrative moment in Game 3 Boston campaign — to be considered when that campaign is developed
- Lupin — The Chant, Gojira

PENDING [PINNED]
- Valkyrie — TBD (shelved until CORYS squad further developed)
- Brick — TBD (shelved until CORYS squad further developed)

COMMERCIAL LICENSING NOTE: All music selections carry commercial licensing flags — acknowledged as future constraint, not immediate creative blocker.

Five of seven scenes fully written with complete dialogue and narrative treatments.
Two scenes (3 and 4) require dedicated development sessions.

KEY DETAILS:
- Scenes 5 and 6 are causally linked — ARES tasks KERAUNOS at end of Zubr sequence
- Scene 7's closing line "American Freedom, over" is a protected narrative beat — the AC-130 crew using Crodyn's terrorist designation back to Romeo over an open military frequency is a small act of institutional defiance with story consequences
- Scene 4 (Red Dawn callback) is also flagged as a standalone trailer/promotional asset

PROJECT WARRIORS — SIDEBAR DEVELOPMENT SUMMARY
Comprehensive record of all story, character, and world-building development
completed in the Project Warriors sidebar/laboratory thread.
================================================================================

STATUS KEY:
[CONFIRMED IN NOTES] = Present in canonical project knowledge files
[SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]  = Developed and agreed in sidebar thread, ready for integration
[PROVISIONAL]        = Sketched but not fully locked — may need revision
[PLANNED / TBD]      = Agreed as planned but placement/details not yet determined
[FLAGGED]            = Gap or continuity risk requiring resolution

Last updated: Current session. Covers all three games and associated world-building.

================================================================================
SECTION 1 — GAME 1 CANONICAL RECORD (CONFIRMED BASELINE)
================================================================================

--- OVERARCHING GAME 1 ---

Title: Project Warriors (series title) [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Setting: Fictional present-day global conflict, 2028 [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Format: Three interconnected campaigns, three protagonists, shared world/timeline
Central event: PANDORA attacks — September 3rd, 2028, nationwide cyber attack
  weaponizing TETHERBREAK program against autonomous military drone systems
PANDORA attack time: First reported 1033 PST. Communications blackout slowed spread.
US Presidential Election: November 3rd, 2028 — exactly two months after PANDORA
Invasion forces: Russian, North Korean, Iranian coalition — amphibious invasion of
  US West Coast. China simultaneously invades and annexes Taiwan. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

--- CAMPAIGN 1: CRITTER SQUAD (ROMEO) ---

Protagonist: LT Ramón "Romeo" Álvarez [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Full name: Ramón Fulgencio Medrano Álvarez [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Unit: Fire Team Delta, US Army 75th Ranger Regiment [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Background: First-generation American of Guatemalan descent. Fluent Spanish speaker.
Nickname origin: Ranger School Selection. Drill sergeant mispronounced his name.
  Romeo said "Me llamo Ramón, cabrón!" with sergeant's back turned. Platoon smoked
  25 minutes. Nickname stuck. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Squad callsigns: Dingo, Howler, Beaver [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

Campaign arc:
Phase 1 — Eastern Europe: Deployed to eastern Poland to shore up NATO border.
  PANDORA triggers Russian encirclement. Delta escapes through southern Poland,
  Czech Republic, Austria to Germany. Regroup at Ramstein Air Base.
Phase 2 — AEGIS infrastructure protection at:
  - Svalbard (main AEGIS datacenter — corrected from Faroe Islands) [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
  - French Alps [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
  - Lemnos, Greece (Aegean Sea) [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
  - Hinderloopen, Netherlands (West Frisian coast) [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Phase 3 — Return to US: Across Brittany to Île Longue French Naval Base.
  Intercept enemy sabotage of French garrison and nuclear submarines Le Terrible
  and Le Vigilant. AEGIS diverted to Maasvlakte Oil and Gas terminal, Rotterdam,
  fighting Russian forces alongside Dutch Marine Corps. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
  Romeo's squad boards nuclear submersible USS District of Columbia.
  Surfaces off Ventura, California due to naval blockade. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Phase 4 — California: Join US Army/Marines clearing Ventura Freeway corridor.
  Enter Los Angeles through North Hollywood.
  Mission "Down Rodeo": Fight through North Hollywood/South Beverly Hills.
    Los Sietes at K Lounge (based on R Bar, 3331 W 8th St, LA) vs 25 DPRK troops.
    Player choices: ignore, flank DPRK, engage LS first, or wait.
    Rare weapon reward: CMMG Mk47 7.62x39mm dropped by Sicario Lieutenant
    (difficult to kill). [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
  Battle of Signal Hill — hold Long Beach Airport. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
  Convoy south to San Diego, Romeo on mounted M2. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
  Final mission: Battle of Coronado Island — repel DPRK/Russian/Iranian amphibious
    assault on North Island Naval Air Station protecting Pacific CSG vessels.

First-game seeding for Game 2 — Romeo's campaign:
  Bisutri seed: K Lounge Sicario Lieutenant speaks unsubtitled Spanish on phone:
    "Ya sé, ya sé. Dile al Bisutrí que el paquete está en Miami. Que lo llame cuando
    esté listo." Romeo understands but player gets no subtitles. Sicario is the
    CMMG Mk47 drop — difficult fight. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
  Glushkin/Tibbets seed: Name "Brent Tibbets / Specter Aerospace" appears on
    conference attendee list in Frankfurt warehouse or peripheral document —
    extremely minimal, designed to be invisible first playthrough. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Red Dawn callback: Enemy paratroopers descending over Smoky Mountains, spotted at
  distance as navigation device. Strong trailer/promotional asset.
  [CONFIRMED AS PLANNED MISSION BEAT]

--- CAMPAIGN 2: DO RIGHT, FEAR NONE (DUCKY) ---

--- CAMPAIGN 3: RIPTIDE RED (SPOOK) ---

Protagonist: CPT Trevor "Spook" Gartner [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Unit: Victor Two Bravo "The Tourists" — CIA Directorate of Operations, Ground Branch
Team: Spook (Gartner), Tripper (Bartlett), Smoke (Oakenfold). Callsign: Noble.
Handler: Senior Case Officer Matthew Mullen, callsign Regent [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
DO: Director Robert Macmillan, later callsign Bishop [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

Mission sequence (confirmed):
  Prologue: Amsterdam → Frankfurt warehouse. Meet Case Officer Cameron Steele
    (Emperor). Briefed on PANDORA and restricted shipment from Turkmenistan.
  Vienna: Hughes (Archduke) at US Embassy. Lebanese cell safehouse in Hernals.
    Team infiltrates empty apartment, woman returns, armed men summoned. Parkour
    chase across rooftops, train platform, underpass. Motorcycles. Beltway chase.
    Spook uses GP SP10A3 Stribog PDW (only time in any campaign — cannot keep).
    Van crashes and explodes. Port of Vienna debrief. Tablet recovered.
  Above My Pay Grade: Navarre house, Frankfurt outskirts. Confront Navarre.
    Laptop yields shipping manifests. Shipment at Warehouse 46. Player can choose
    to give Navarre/Budanova new identities (Navarre calls to say goodbye if yes).
  Frankfurt Warehouse 46: Atlas personnel. Shipment already moved. Tripper recovers
    hard drive. Team destroys warehouse. PYTHIA contact Jaeger Stanzler helps match
    partial schedule to chartered flights.
  Infrastructure Day: Abu Dhabi, GenCorp skyscraper. Rappel to data center.
    Shipment linked to Agarwal Berkhan. Optional target: Leandro Blommaert.
  Man From Medan / DRAGONSLAYER: Medan City, Indonesia. Lestari House compound.
    Berkhan escapes via Mi-8 helicopter. Spook rips security ID from belt, uses it
    to lift lockdown. Berkhan's helicopter hit by "malfunctioning" Skynex RADS
    (actually TETHERBREAK sabotage). Berkhan killed. Macmillan contacts team —
    Regent "urgently reassigned." New handler: Bishop/Macmillan. Operation WHITEOUT.
  Pandora's Box: Miami Beach, Desautels Resort Hotel. Los Sietes + KYSC inside.
    KYSC = brainwashed Montoya Farm victims with CogniConnect implants. Deliberate
    Goldberg/Macmillan trap. Team defeats KYSC, destroys PANDORA device. KYSC have
    MKULTRA-linked tattoos pointing to Montoya Farm. Helicopter attack. Elite sicario
    ambush. 2-ton fertilizer bomb. Elevator cable escape. Parking garage fight.
    Exit 300ft from destroyed hotel as first responders arrive.
  Burning Daylight: Montoya Farm, near San Rafael, New Mexico. U-Haul infiltration.
    Directional mic on Stockbridge. Keycard from gala event ballroom. Security room.
    Underground complex: prison, medical facility, dormitories, simulated sky plaza,
    "movie set" rooms (snuff production), MKULTRA symbols.
    Collectible: Hidden vent — man hosing blood off operating table.
    Collectible: Locked Ludovico Room — brainwashing facility, treatment logs visible.
    MAWL-DA collectible: Found in locked Pelican case in underground complex.
      Presence indicates serious US military equipment access. Story beat. [CONFIRMED]
    Server room: Tripper plants hardware implant. Extracts encrypted data. Exfil via
      laundry room shaft behind filing cabinet.
    Decrypted data: Massive kompromat-trafficking-dark money architecture. FSB,
      Mossad, IRGC, Chinese MSS, DPRK State Intelligence, NATO apparatus all involved.
      Tripper: "Holy mother of God! Looks like everybody and their mother-in-law is
      on this motherfucker's payroll." FinBud/crypto links to KINGMAKER/Goldberg.
      Buried CIA report on Riptide Red (document itself purged). NSA op DARMA.
  Come Fly With Me: St. Croix, US Virgin Islands (near Anguilla). ~40 miles south
    of East McFarlane Island (Caribbean — fictionalized Little St. James Island).
    Wait for nightfall/weather. Acquire Found BFA-2 floatplane from coastal compound.
    Smoke flies team dark, engine off. Land at small cove.
  Sins of Our Fathers: East McFarlane Island. Evidence of trafficking, illegal
    pornography, cannibalism, ritual human sacrifice in underground complex.
    War Wolves dispatched by Stockbridge: three Tier 1 operators, dark grey gear,
    Kevlar wolf masks, CFIM-equipped CogniConnect implant stacks that trigger
    terminal counter-forensic detonation on death.
    Callsigns: Crimson One, Two, Three. Must be defeated before reaching helipad.
    Team corners Goldberg at helipad. Stockbridge preparing airlift. Macmillan
    orders stand down, gives Goldberg safe passage. Victor Two Bravo declared rogue.
    Cliffhanger ending of Game 1. PANDORA attacks happen simultaneously.
    Goldberg quote (gives final mission its name): "Spend enough time doing what I
    do, and you begin to see it for what it is. An empire built on the sins of our
    fathers that keeps them alive to haunt their children. To remind them of their
    place. Of who they are and of what they must do." [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

First-game seeding for Game 2 — Spook's campaign:
  Bisutri seed 1: Pandora's Box mission dossier — Los Sietes personnel section lists
    Lozada-Arias, Edgar Murillo / "Bisutri" / Operations Deputy CLSO Gulf Command.

--- GAME 2 OVERARCHING ---

Setting: Continuation of global conflict. Russian occupation of US East Coast and
  interior. Russian Baltic offensive in Europe. China having annexed Taiwan,
  moving on South Asia, Middle East. Opening South Pacific front (Australia).
  US Air Force partially degraded by PANDORA cyber effects — network-dependent
  F-22s/F-35s compromised; legacy platforms (A-10 Warthog) operationally relevant
  due to PANDORA resilience and Crodyn administration's military mismanagement.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Timeline: Immediately following Game 1. Specific inter-game time gap TBD. [FLAGGED]

Three campaigns: Three interconnected stories, convergent event touches all simultaneously.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

CONVERGENT EVENT — Presidential Address: Crodyn names AFC as domestic terrorist
  organization under 18 USC. Names LT Ramón Álvarez by name as rogue officer.
  Claims AFC coordinates with foreign intelligence. 30-day voluntary disengagement
  window. Framed as protecting wartime constitutional order. Affirmed by SCOTUS
  Justices Howard (fictionalized Clarence Thomas) and Pedilla (fictionalized Samuel
  Alito). Structural lynchpin connecting all three campaigns. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
  Full address text written. Available in sidebar thread.

UNHMNA: United Nations Humanitarian Mission to North America. White UN vehicles,
  blue helmets, foreign troops in American environments. Hospital ships Dawn of
  Mercy and Beacon of Hope. Jarring visual juxtaposition — imagery historically
  associated with developing-world conflicts now in American suburban landscapes.
  [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

--- CAMPAIGN 1: AMERICAN FREEDOM (ROMEO) ---

Campaign subtitle: "War Hits Home" [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Teaser tagline: "War Hits Home. American Freedom." [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Teaser music: Jesse Welles, "Good Morning, America" — mixed choir arrangement
  closes the trailer. Subliminal number station fragment (Russian, 2 seconds) buried
  under choir's final note decay — connects to Glushkin/Persistent Threat trailer.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED — FULL TRAILER CONCEPT DEVELOPED]

Opening cinematic: Camera at roof height over Calloway, KY main street. Early morning.
  Jesse Welles song plays. Russian flags, troops, roadblocks. Burnt-out houses.
  Civilians combing wreckage. Foreign occupation vs familiar American landscape.
  Designed to feel surreal. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES / SIDEBAR CONFIRMED — FULL SCENE WRITTEN]

Primary setting: Calloway, Kentucky, Harlan County. Nearby community: Redbud. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Occupation timeline: Campaign begins approximately Day 31 of Calloway occupation.

--- ACT ONE: "GOOD MORNING, AMERICA" ---

RESISTANCE CELL CHARACTERS:

Dale Pruett — Age 54. Third-generation pharmacist/owner, Pruett Family Pharmacy est. 1887.
  Town's informal civic backbone. Organized resistance cell. Daughter Kelsey Pruett
  detained Day 8. Primary Romeo-civilian interface. Logistics, local intel, coordination.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Renata Voss — Age 47. Former Superintendent, Harlan County School District.
  Composed, methodical, politically skilled. Organized food/medicine distribution from
  Day 4. Held 6 hours by occupation Day 12, released, did not change activities.
  Communications, civilian network, information management. Carries handwritten list
  of 43 unaccounted-for children from her district. Post-Second Level confrontation
  with Romeo: controlled, devastating. Does not forgive easily. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Cody Beaumont — Age 23. Former volunteer firefighter/part-time mechanic. Friend
  Marcus killed at checkpoint Day 6. Knows every road, trail, field, drainage ditch
  within ten-mile radius. Can repair most vehicles. Grief-driven urgency — volatile.
  Romeo's ground-level partner for field operations.
  TRAGIC HERO ARC: Dies during Second Level detainee rescue. Heroic death enables
  Kelsey Pruett's escape but Cody is captured and killed by FSB-attached occupation
  personnel. Death never explicitly described or confirmed in dialogue — implied only.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Frank Kowalski — Age 67. Former SSgt, 82nd Airborne. Two tours. Retired, owns hardware
  store. Military advisor to cell. Bridge between Romeo and civilians. Quiet, watches
  everything, says little. Key private counsel to Romeo. Captured during AMBITIOUS
  operation — held 6 hours, extracted by Romeo and Priya's unit from informal FSB
  processing facility in Harlan outskirts. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Gene Marlow — 50s. Feed delivery driver, Redbud. Twice-weekly checkpoint runs.
  Knows every farm road between Calloway and county line. Recruited as logistics asset.
  Runs supply route to weapons cache and AFC network. Interrogated by Glushkin at
  checkpoint (Low Ground mission). Eventually burned as route asset when occupation
  tightens after presidential address. Final scene: "Tell me when it's over. I'll
  drive through that checkpoint one more time." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

CODY'S DEATH — LOADING SCREEN IMAGE:
  Young male, late 20s, deceased, suspended by neck from highway gantry. Cardboard
  plaque in Russian Cyrillic and English: "An American traitor to the Russian Federation
  who conspired with the enemy to lead American soldiers on to Russian positions and
  helped them cruelly murder brave Russian men. May his death be a warning to those
  who seek to follow his ways." References Calloway and Redbud communities. Never
  explicitly identified as Cody. Connection implied, strategically ambiguous, left for
  player to make. Appears exactly once — loading screen immediately preceding mission
  following Romeo learning of Cody's fate. Never repeated. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES /
  SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

ACT ONE MISSIONS:

Mission "Low Ground" — Pre-dawn recon, Romeo + Cody. Water tower observation.
  Discovers: third BTR behind Elks Lodge, staggered patrols, signals monitoring KAMAZ
  truck at agricultural office, six covered civilian vehicles from Redbud at medical
  clinic parking structure. South road checkpoint — Glushkin's unmarked officer
  interrogates Gene Marlow. First player glimpse of Glushkin. Culvert route identified.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Dead Air" — Two options: disable signals vehicle (appears as equipment failure)
  or neutralize crew member during rotation (triggers disruption window). Communications
  window established. Romeo contacts command. Learns: Calloway is designated priority
  insurgency support zone; weapons cache pre-positioned seven miles southeast; Calloway
  is first cell in what must become a network. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "The Redbud Vehicles" — Romeo + Cody reconnoiter medical clinic parking structure.
  14+ civilian detainees behind temporary barriers. Cody identifies Kelsey Pruett.
  Restrains himself. Returns to pharmacy. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Farm Road" — Contact with Gene Marlow at grain elevator pull-off. Cody first
  approach, Romeo exits tree line. Marlow agrees to help. Weapons cache at abandoned
  Henderson farm seven miles southeast. Cache contents: four M4A1 suppressors, two M110
  semi-auto sniper systems, sidearms, ammo, fragmentation grenades, breaching charges,
  trauma-grade medical supplies, two NVG sets, encrypted tactical radio.
  Handwritten note: "For whoever finds this — you're not alone. Get to work."
  Cody keeps the note. Cache moved through checkpoint in Marlow's truck under
  Glushkin's contact's observation — tense checkpoint sequence. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Second Level" — Detainee rescue from medical clinic parking structure.
  Romeo takes ground floor guard. Cody holds stairwell. 14 civilians extracted including
  Kelsey Pruett. Withdrawal through alleys toward culvert. Enemy patrol interception —
  Cody covers civilians from exposed position, holds too long, shot and captured.
  Romeo reaches him: 14 seconds. Cody's last words: "Tell my uncle's friend — tell him
  I said it was worth it." Dale sees Kelsey at culvert — no dialogue, two seconds on
  screen. 14 civilians reach Marlow's truck. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Post-Second Level — Renata confrontation: Controlled, precise accounting of what Cody's
  death cost. "I need you to tell me — whether there was a version of that operation where
  he came home." Romeo: "I hear you." No resolution. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Frank's response to Cody: "Kid was good people. Let's make sure it meant something."
  Returns immediately to map. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

ACT ONE — ADDITIONAL CHARACTER BEATS:
  Aldridge — Former county sheriff's deputy, encountered among Second Level rescued
  detainees. Joins cell. Becomes significant operational asset. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

AFC FOUNDING:
  Frequency mission coordination — multiple cells on same frequency simultaneously for
  first time. Terrell Washington suggests "American Freedom something." Romeo: "American
  Freedom Corps." Washington: "Yeah. That works." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

NETWORK EXPANSION CONTACTS:
  Patrice Odom — Barbourville. Former county emergency management coordinator. Kept
    American flag folded in coat for two months — couldn't let occupation have it.
    Gave flag to Aldridge for Elks Lodge recapture. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
  Terrell Washington — Cumberland. High school football coach. AFC naming contribution.

    suspended but intact. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

    Romeo has encountered. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
  Dills — Priya's wary unit member. Signs on after Romeo's honest answer about risk.
    [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

ACT TWO MISSIONS:

Mission "Long View" — Ridge above Cumberland Gap. Squad reunion scene. Dingo: "You grew
  a beard." Romeo: "Yeah." Dingo: "Looks bad." Romeo: "I know." Dingo: "Good to have
  you back, boss." 12-minute patrol gap at bridge mile marker seven identified.

Mission "Supply and Demand" — Coordinated supply corridor interdiction. Three elements.
  Romeo/Howler on bridge. Dingo with Terrell Washington's people. Beaver coordinates.
  Corridor dark 81 hours. Glushkin's response too precise — Aldridge: "He's not chasing
  us. He's mapping us."

Mission "Other Towns" — Three contact vignettes: Hargrove (documentation, constitutional
  question), Priya Okonkwo ("What took you so long?"), Middlesboro group declined —

Mission "Glushkin's Map" — Glushkin exploits Middlesboro thread. Counter-intelligence
  operation. Leak identified and closed via Marlow's warning. Middlesboro group burned.

Mission "Priya's Ground" — Romeo/Howler embedded with Priya's unit two days. Dills
  character. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Breaking Signal" (planning) — Operation AMBITIOUS designed. Five cells, Priya's

  Aldridge's response: "Well. That's ambitious." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Ambitious — Part One: Dark" — Communications interdiction phase. All elements
  simultaneous. Dingo: "Too clean." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Ambitious — Part Two: Signal" — Priya assaults courthouse, Harlan. Data

Mission "Ambitious — Part Three: Cost" — Frank captured. Romeo + Priya rescue Frank

  "Yes." Frank: "Good. Then it was worth it." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Neighbor" — First contact outside Calloway. Romeo + Aldridge to Harlan proper.

Mission "Three Counties" — Montage structure. Ten days, six cells across three counties.

Mission "Frequency" — AFC's first coordinated operation. Three cells simultaneously.

Mission "American Freedom" — Largest AFC offensive. Target: occupation's primary
  logistics hub, Harlan County fairgrounds. Five cells. Romeo commands from mobile

Mission "Hargrove's Record" — Documentation moved out via Marlow's route. Reaches

Mission "Washington's Wall" — Increased scrutiny of Cumberland school. Romeo moves AFC

Mission "High Ground" — Joint operation with 101st Airborne (Captain Lassiter) pushing
  north from Tennessee. First contact with conventional US forces. Garrison falls.

THE WARTIME PRESIDENTIAL ADDRESS — ROMEO'S PERSPECTIVE:

GLUSHKIN ARC IN ROMEO'S CAMPAIGN:

Face to Face (optional mission) — Romeo goes to grain elevator pull-off at Glushkin's
  invitation. Two men acknowledge each other across the line. Glushkin: "Yes. I do
  know why it's worth fighting for." Drives away. Aldridge: "What was that?" Romeo:
  "Recon. For both of us." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  Tibbets/Glushkin in collectibles. File culminates in full Glushkin activation scene

Glushkin's burning call — Number station, 2341 hours. Sequence: 8-3-1-6-5-0-2-7-4-1.
  Glushkin writes "Понятно" (Understood) in notebook. Keeps folded page.
  Walks out into occupation's night — chooses how his story ends, not Lipnin's decision.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED — FULL SCENE WRITTEN]

Glushkin's final words to Romeo (delivered in slight natural Russian accent):
  "I only did what I had to do. And I know exactly what it cost. Every single time.
  And I would have done it again, if I knew I had to. But now it is over, and it is
  time that you do what you must. You and I both know there is no other way, Álvarez.

Campaign ending: Romeo watches US Army vehicles move through liberated town. Terrell
  Washington on radio: "You seeing this?" Romeo: "Yeah." Washington: "Good morning,

Game 3 seeds in Romeo's campaign:
  Seed 1: Encrypted communication from command contains buried line: "Regent sends
    regards." First indirect connection between Romeo and Spook storylines.
  Seed 2: Hargrove asks Romeo what the AFC becomes after the occupation ends. Romeo

--- CAMPAIGN 2: PERSISTENT THREAT (DUCKY) ---

Campaign subtitle: "The System Fell. We Didn't." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Final title: PERSISTENT THREAT (formerly working title AEGIS Falls — that title
  reserved as mission name within campaign) [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Teaser tagline: "We Are Taking Our Home Back. AEGIS Falls." [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Teaser music: "Kyiv" by Apashe featuring Alina Pash [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

TACTICAL LAYER MISSIONS:

Mission "Cold Open" — Norwegian coastal town exfiltration under fire. Russian naval
  infantry landing. AEGIS fighting withdrawal to helicopter pickup. Links up with
  Norwegian coastal defense unit. Switchblade saves elderly Norwegian civilian —
  45 seconds, doesn't break mission. Conversation about this happens later.
  Walker on DAOG net: "Good exfil. We have a problem." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Dead Frequency" — EW node interdiction, converted NATO facility, northern
  Estonia. Two-element assault: CORYS secures northern approach, AEGIS penetrates
  facility. Four-hundred-meter river crossing under Frost overwatch. Valkyrie:
  "I've seen Frost work. It's appropriate faith." EW equipment destroyed. Lupin
  photographs technical parameters document before destroying. Brick takes
  through-and-through wound to left forearm. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Hard Winter" — Mobile EW convoy tracking, Latvian interior. Two in-game days.
  Three gameplay moments: movement establishing terrain, near-miss patrol encounter,
  frozen reservoir crossing. Halliday on comms: "I can't give you certainty." Ducky:
  "Nobody ever can." Convoy destroyed. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Permafrost" (formerly Cold Frontier — renamed to avoid confusion with Frost
  backstory mission "Cold Frontier 07") — Svalbard. Third EW node. Pre-positioned for
  direct attack on AEGIS datacenter. Halliday: "They're waiting for authorization."
  Vympel security element. Frost on ice shelf — Ducky pulls him off before flanked.
  Frost: "I had them." Ducky: "I know. Keep moving." Node destroyed in sequence —
  line cut first, then equipment. Lupin takes fragment wound to shoulder.
  Sea exfil via rigid inflatable to Norwegian Coast Guard vessel.
  Walker: "That's the good news." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "Hull Breach" (corrected from "Hill Breach" — typo noted and fixed) —
  Kaliningrad harbor. Russian intelligence vessel Akademik Volkov. AEGIS + Nereid Black
  joint operation. Submarine approach via USS District of Columbia. Harbor patrol forces
  six-minute hold on bottom. Rime breaches plated access point in 4 min 17 sec.
  CQB through vessel interior. Data infrastructure destroyed. Lupin handles intel
  exploitation despite shoulder wound. Rime scuttles vessel. Undertow exits last.
  Akademik Volkov sinks as apparent accident. Recovered drive contains DAOG credential
  identifier fragment — ZEUS level, Tremblay. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

INVESTIGATIVE THREAD BEATS:

Beat 1 "The Parameters" — Dead Frequency technical document reveals AEGIS internal
  system nomenclature used by Russian EW team — confirming inside access. Halliday
  produces list of seven senior DAOG personnel with AEGIS architecture access.
  Eliminates one (Brussels only, remote access). Four remain. Access anomalies trace
  back 18 months minimum. Ducky: "That's not a leak. That's an agent." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Beat 2 "The Architecture" — Hard Winter quiet period. Halliday traces AEGIS development
  contracts. Core technology licensing traces to Nexus Meridian Holdings (Cayman
  Islands). Nexus Meridian appears in Montoya Farm financial records — transfers made
  14 months before first AEGIS licensing agreement. AEGIS architecture partly funded
  through KINGMAKER-connected financial infrastructure. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Beat 3 "The Credential" — Akademik Volkov drive completes credential identifier —
  ZEUS-level, Tremblay's personal authentication token including biometric profile.
  18 months of access. Halliday: "I wish we were wrong." Decision to take to Walker
  through back channel outside DAOG communications architecture. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Beat 4 "What Ducky Does With It" — 0200 conversation post-Hull Breach. Decision to take
  to Walker via Halliday's counterintelligence node channel. Walker confirms he's known
  something was wrong. "Now you've given me enough." Walker tasks unauthorized mission:
  find Tremblay, confront with evidence, secure confession or defection.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Mission "AEGIS Falls" — Aix-en-Provence, southern France. Private estate, GenCorp-
  connected holding company. AEGIS alone. Ducky finds Tremblay in study. Full
  conversation — European strategic autonomy ideology, FSB finding architectural backdoor
  independently, Tremblay's attempt to manage rather than report, waiting for something
  to change. Tremblay: "AEGIS falls regardless." Ducky: "Then we build something better."
  Tremblay agrees to Walker's process. Conditions include Crodyn not protected.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

SQUAD CHARACTER MOMENTS:
  Frost and Jussi: 0300 in operations room. Two coffees. Frost: "The cold helps.
    It's quieter in my head." Mentions Jussi Mustonen by name — only time in sequel.
  Switchblade/Norwegian civilian conversation: Ducky's threshold was 45 seconds —
    clean, no comment. 60 seconds — he would have said something.
  Lupin/Brick wound exchange: "It's fine." "Sure." "It's fine." "I heard you." "Good."
  Valkyrie/Brick re Hull Breach: Brick wants in. Ducky: "He's holding the perimeter
    with Valkyrie. That's not a lesser role." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

ADDRESS LANDING — DUCKY'S PERSPECTIVE:
  0347 hours. Halliday wakes Ducky with tablet. Reads full address text. Ducky and
  Halliday discuss — Ducky identifies address as Crodyn demonstrating panic not control.
  0600 command call: Walker reads DAOG legal position (address inapplicable to NATO
  mandate). Tremblay: "Exercise discretion." Tremblay's pause after specific phrasing
  becomes investigative data point for Halliday. Tremblay received address before command
  call — implies advance knowledge from Crodyn's circle. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

--- CAMPAIGN 3: GODKILLER (SPOOK) ---

Campaign subtitle: "You Can't Kill a Dead Man" [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Teaser tagline: "How Do You Kill A Man Who's Already Dead? Godkiller." [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Teaser music: "King Nothing" by Metallica [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

OPENING SITUATION:
  Victor Two Bravo declared rogue. Six weeks since PANDORA attacks. Spook repositioned,
  secured channels, built operational picture. Fort Lauderdale safehouse.
  Coleman Federal facility admin contact surfaces — processed unusual medical transfer
  for Goldberg night of breakout. Duty officer was Douglas Paul Nasmith (actually
  Grigoryi Pavlovich Lebedev — FSB illegal, Boston City Hall Finance). Transfer covered
  by Meridian Shield Services tracing to GenCorp-connected holding company. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

COLEMAN EXTRACTION MECHANISM:
  El Furtivo (Pablo Ignacio Hernández Díaz) leads noisy Los Sietes extraction through
  prison cell block, causing mass damage. Simultaneously, second team plants mutilated
  DNA-contaminated corpse as "Goldberg" in open cell. Goldberg moved to medical bay,
  placed in coffin-like oblong box, loaded into hearse by bribed COs. Convoy exfiltrates
  during riot chaos. Goldberg declared dead. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

THREE-TRACK STRUCTURE:
  Track 1 (Spook): Protecting Budanova and hunting Goldberg.
  Track 2 (Tripper): Intelligence manipulation via Montoya Farm persistent access.
    Contact with Hartwell (NSA analyst, DARMA operation, Vela 2 knowledge).
  Track 3 (Smoke): Supporting resistance organizations including AFC network (unknowingly).
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Smoke-AFC connection: Smoke realizes AFC is network he's been supplying when address
  names Romeo. Tells Spook. Supply route kept open. Romeo never knows who's on the
  other end. "American Freedom." "Then yes. Keep it open." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

KEY MISSIONS:
  "The Wasp's Nest" — Oaxaca, Mexico. Spook approaches La Avispa openly (deliberate).
    Restaurant meeting, midday. She was already there. Knows he's CIA. La Avispa has
    lead on Goldberg's location — won't give it, will take him there personally.
    "I've been looking for interesting work." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  "Dead Letters" — Cuba, Miramar. Los Sietes financial officer Cristóbal Reyes.
    La Avispa vouches approach. Reyes gives Goldberg's first movement (Florida airstrip
    to Bahamas). Gives financial transfer document confirming Meridian Shield/GenCorp.
    [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  "Ghost Signal" — Tripper's track, player controls Tripper only time in campaign.
    Contact and authentication with Hartwell via Montoya Farm access. Vela 2 fragment
    revealed — connected to near-miss nuclear incident used as conspiracy leverage.
    Full details parceled across remaining missions. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  "Safe House" — Budanova protection and relocation. Meridian Shield surveillance
    on her location. La Avispa negotiates extended Los Sietes protection with El Tiburón
    — doesn't disclose terms. "A favor. For later. The kind that won't cost you anything."
    Budanova: "He said if you ever met you, you were one of the ones who wasn't owned."
    [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  "Haverford" — Panama City, Panama. Financial institution/dark money clearing house.
    Spook + La Avispa first two-person operation. Financial trail leads to Caribbean.
    Goldberg positioned waiting for Crodyn's communication. La Avispa tells Spook about
    El Tiburón favor. "You're a strange man, Gartner." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  "Regent" — Regent reunion. Two operations built same case from different ends.
    Regent has Hartwell knowledge (14 months). Senate Intelligence Committee contact
    established. Goldberg's 72-hour window before Crodyn communication arrives.
    "I wondered how long it would take you." "It holds." "Go get him." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  "Come Fly With Me" — St. Croix, US Virgin Islands (Caribbean). ~40 miles south
    of East McFarlane Island. Acquire Found BFA-2 floatplane. Smoke flies team dark.
    La Avispa present. Quiet scene before departure. "Ask me again someday." "Someday."
    [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED / CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

  "Sins of Our Fathers" (Godkiller) — East McFarlane Island. War Wolves. La Avispa
    handles Crimson Three. Goldberg cornered at helipad. Stockbridge steps back.
    Goldberg: "Spend enough time doing what I do..." Spook: "So the sins of the fathers
    are yours now. What do you want to do with them?" Goldberg agrees to process.
    Macmillan contacts Spook — Spook demands authorization code, invokes Senate Intel
    Committee oversight. Macmillan goes dark. Goldberg in custody. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Campaign ending: Goldberg in process. Tremblay in Walker's accounting. Budanova and
  Hartwell on record. Crodyn's communication intercepted — becomes evidentiary record.
  Text from unsaved number: "Ask me again." Regent: "We need you on a call." Spook:
  "Give me a minute... Okay. I'm ready." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

ADDRESS LANDING — SPOOK'S PERSPECTIVE:
  Spook watches address live, alone. The three other team members give him the room.
  Hears Romeo named. Identifies address as panic dressed as damage control. Accelerant
  for Goldberg hunt — window closing. Decides to find La Avispa first. Smoke confirms
  he's been supplying AFC unknowingly. Route stays open. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

--- GAME 2 CROSS-CAMPAIGN CONNECTIONS ---

All three campaigns experience presidential address simultaneously from different positions.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED — FULL CONVERGENT EVENT WRITTEN WITH ALL THREE PERSPECTIVE SCENES]

Romeo-Spook connection: Smoke's Track Three uses AFC infrastructure. Romeo eventually
  aware someone outside his chain is using his network, chooses not to push back.
  Neither knows the other's full picture. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Ducky-Spook connection: Tripper's intelligence manipulation produces document reaching
  Halliday through unaccountable channel. Both pulling same thread from different ends.
  [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Tremblay-Goldberg-GenCorp connection: AEGIS architectural compromise and GenCorp-Nexus
  Meridian financial architecture connect to same shadow network Spook is unraveling.
  Ducky's discovery becomes part of wider evidentiary record. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

--- GLUSHKIN / VYACHESLAV TIMOFEEVICH GLUSHKIN ---
Cover identity: Brent Henry Tibbets, aerospace electrical engineer, Haverhill MA
Cover employer: Specter Aerospace, Peabody MA
Cover education: MIT — electrical engineering and aeronautics, completed by age 29
Real background: Born 1982, Volgodonsk, Rostov Oblast, RSFSR. MGIMO degree
  (Translation, Linguistics, Cross-Cultural Communication, English and Mandarin).
  18 months clandestine linguistics training, Korolyov near Moscow. 18 months FSB
  officer training, Academy of the Russian Federal Security Service, Moscow.
  Ghost identity: Real Brent Tibbets was 24-year-old homeless substance-addicted man
  from Haverhill MA, no known relatives, disappeared without report approximately 9
  months before Glushkin's assignment. Body likely misidentified or buried as John Doe.
  No death certificate exists. Case remains open. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Languages: Russian (native), English, Mandarin, Arabic, Spanish, Portuguese, French,
  Greek, German, Farsi (all fluent). Conversational Chechen. Scholarly ancient Greek
  and Latin. History of English and Chinese languages. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Skills: Semi-competitive chess player. Proficient with Russian military infantry weapons.
Archetype: Christoph Waltz / Inglourious Basterds — Landa archetype but with distinct
  internal logic. Sophisticated, charming, intelligent, composed — but with decisive
  killer instinct. Genuine internal belief system (not pure ideology). Recognizes
  capability in Romeo. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Activation: June 4th, 2028 (91 days before PANDORA attacks). Activated by Lebedev
  (Nasmith) in his Specter Aerospace office. Sara Teasdale poem "Redbirds" (first
  word: Redbud — deliberate, per Lipnin's knowledge of Glushkin's operational
  territory). Full activation scene written. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED — FULL SCENE WRITTEN]
Authentication phrase from Lebedev: "Have a good one." (Chosen for maximum invisibility
  in American vernacular, universal usage, haunting recognition quality for players
  who hear it in real life post-game.) [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Burning call: Number station, Sequence 8-3-1-6-5-0-2-7-4-1. Writes "Понятно" in
  notebook. Keeps folded page — one act of private ownership. Chooses Romeo over
  Lipnin. Full burning call scene written. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED — FULL SCENE WRITTEN]
Final words: Delivered in slight natural Russian accent (cover dropped). "I only did
  what I had to do. And I know exactly what it cost. Every single time. And I would
  have done it again, if I knew I had to. But now it is over, and it is time that you
  do what you must. You and I both know there is no other way, Álvarez. It's the end
  of the road. It had to happen one day." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Game 1 seeding: Conference attendee list, Frankfurt (Brent Tibbets/Specter Aerospace).
  Bastion Infotech contact record on Navarre's laptop (Tibbets, B.). Ghost signal in
  Wirecutter signals overlay (Massachusetts origin, unresolved). [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

--- LEBEDEV / DOUGLAS PAUL NASMITH ---
Real name: Grigoryi Pavlovich Lebedev
Born: March 11, 1970, Nizhny Novgorod, USSR. Age 58 in story timeline.
Cover: Douglas Paul Nasmith, Russian economist
Position: Head of Finance department, Boston City Hall (33 years in cover)
Role: Activated 3 months before PANDORA attacks to gather Boston infrastructure

  chokepoints — for FSB invasion planning. Activated Glushkin upon receiving order.
Appearance: Thin, salt-and-pepper hair, round wire-frame glasses slightly too small

  has the seams of manufactured fluency that only someone else with manufactured
  fluency (like Glushkin) would notice. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

  Harder to remove than a field agent. Third-game version of the Tremblay problem.
  [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3]

--- LIPNIN / GENNADIY FYODOROVICH LIPNIN ---
Background: Very high-ranking KGB officer, continued into FSB after Soviet collapse.

  headquarters, Moscow. Close daily oversight of assets and operational officers.
  Documented history of burning compromised assets — not reassigning, eliminating.
  Personally recruited Glushkin in 1995 (at age 23 after MGIMO graduation).
Born: Mid-to-late 1950s (estimate). KGB from mid-1970s. Survived multiple political
  systems by positioning correctly.
Glushkin/Lipnin dynamic: Glushkin knew Lipnin would burn him once the assignment

SECTION 4 — WORLD-BUILDING AND CONSPIRACY ARCHITECTURE
================================================================================

--- CONSPIRACY STRUCTURE ---

PANDORA: Suppressed CIA operational plan to weaponize TETHERBREAK on US soil.
  Most records purged. Remainder archived in cryptically labeled box, deep storage.
  [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

TETHERBREAK: Top-secret CIA program to develop means of unauthorized access to US
  strategic military C&C infrastructure and taking control of autonomous multi-domain
  weapons systems. Started as penetration test / insurance policy against the Pentagon
  becoming reckless. Evolved into false flag tool when Crodyn's criminal history
  threatened exposure. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

KINGMAKER: World's most powerful kompromat/blackmail resource. Operated by rotating
  "KINGMAKER" figure — Goldberg currently. Co-operated with Gillian Stockbridge
  (CHAPERONE). Role changed hands periodically but operation continued.
  Involvement from: FSB, Mossad, IRGC, Chinese MSS, DPRK State Intelligence, NATO
  security apparatus, various non-state entities. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

RIPTIDE RED: Deep-state conspiracy that planned and executed PANDORA attacks, framed
  as Chinese cyberattack. Enabled: Crodyn's unconstitutional 3rd term, suspension of
  2028 election, domestic security crackdown, suspension of habeas corpus.
  [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

DARMA: NSA operation to conceal evidence and suppress inquiry about conspiracy-
  affiliated activities. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

SPRINGBLOAT: Compromised DHS/NSA operation to suppress domestic communications about
  and inquiries into the PANDORA attack. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

Shadow Underground (various names — The Forever Pact, Eternal Society, Eclipse Society,
  The Founders, The Delta Project, The Illuminati): Global human trafficking/kompromat/
  dark money operation beneath the visible conspiracy. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

GenCorp (Global Executive Network Corporation): American multinational surveillance
  data and defense ICT solutions provider. Connected to KINGMAKER financial architecture
  through Nexus Meridian Holdings → AEGIS development funding. Berkhan (largest
  shareholder ~25%), Crodyn, and Ruetger all hold stock. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

Palisade Systems: US defense contractor, ties to Israel. "Drone countermeasure"
  technology recipient from Bastion Infotech. Owned by Paul Ruetger, headed by
  David Bass. (Fictionalized Palantir.) [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

Atlas Solutions: Global PMC based in Singapore. Recently contracted for GenCorp
  operations security. Connected to former Israeli defense minister Eliezer Baruch
  Yadat. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

Not playable faction in Game 1. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Grim: Squad leader. Cold, exact, unflinching, better when the plan fails.
Rime: Technical breach specialist.
Lantern: Observation and pattern recognition.
Undertow: Last one out. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Game 2 return: Hull Breach mission, Akademik Volkov, Kaliningrad harbor. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

--- LOS SIETES CARTEL ---

El Cártel de Los Sietes de Oaxaca (CLSO). Leader: Carlos Miguel Mencia de Vargas,
  "El Tiburón." Skeletal shark jaw tattoo on chin/neck. Not in-game, dossier only.
Edgar Murillo "Bisutri" Lozada-Arias — El Tiburón's second-in-command. Operations
  deputy. "Bisutri" = scalpel (Spanish). Surgical, precise, efficient methodology.
  Leads Coleman prison extraction operation in Game 2. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]
Pablo Ignacio "El Furtivo" Hernández Díaz — High-ranking Los Sietes-affiliated human
  trafficker. Goldberg associate. Gets broken out of Sumterville simultaneously with
  (and as cover for) Goldberg's extraction. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]
Yelena Volkova "La Avispa" — Former FSB, now Los Sietes enforcer/tracker. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

================================================================================
SECTION 5 — GAME 3 SEEDS AND PROVISIONAL DEVELOPMENT
================================================================================

NOTE: Game 3 is not yet mapped. All below is provisional — seeds planted in Games 1/2,
sketches discussed for future development.

--- CONFIRMED GAME 3 SEEDS ---

Nuclear event (Option Two from convergent event discussion): Reserved for Game 3.
  Too large to spend in Game 2. Third game can be built around it as central dramatic
  reality. Vela 2 (suppressed near-miss nuclear incident) connects here. [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3]

Tremblay ambiguity in Game 1 and 2: Fully resolved by end of Game 2. Third game
  inherits question of what replaces AEGIS and who controls it. [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3]

Macmillan: Role in conspiracy documented but not yet publicly accountable. Goes dark
  after Spook invokes Senate Intel Committee. Third game's most important unresolved
  antagonist. [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3]

AFC's future: What does the AFC become post-occupation? Who controls it? Who tries to
  use it? Hargrove's question to Romeo: "You should think about it. Because someone
  else will, if you don't." Romeo's Game 3 throughline. [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3]

Regent's "Godkiller" speech: "The gods they killed weren't divine. They just had enough
  power that everyone agreed to pretend they were." Framework for Game 3 institutional
  reckoning. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

--- GAME 3 ROMEO — BOSTON CAMPAIGN SKETCH ---

Status: Very early sketch. No confirmed structure yet.

Setting: Boston urban combat. Diverse terrain — suburbs, built-up areas, multiple
  types. Narrative bridge from Kentucky to Massachusetts needed. [PROVISIONAL]

Van Hult side quest — Mitchell Van Hult: Former USAF technician, mid-50s. Ran body
  shop in Boston. Occupation seized shop, converted to motor pool/vehicle maintenance.
  Built armored bulldozer ("Killdozer" reference — subtle, never named, detail reward
  for players who know the real-world lore) in parking garage with scrounged/volunteered
  equipment. Neighborhood-scale liberation arc: breach Russian command post/checkpoint
  with bulldozer; progressive block liberation; final mission reclaims Van Hult's shop.
  [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3 SKETCH]

A-10 Warthog scene ("THUNDERBOLT flight"): Romeo element intercepts Russian armor
  column (reinforcements for resistance suppression) on suburban entry road.
  Player on foot throughout, IFV/APC used for cover, open hatch for reveal moment.
  "Romeo, listen. You hear that?" Radio call. Soft focus pull upward.
  First BRRT arrives before aircraft visible — rounds hit first, cannon report after.
  A-10 pulls off run, visible now, banking for second pass. Second BRRT. Column
  suppressed. Mission: Crew: "Road's yours." [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3 SKETCH]
  A-10 operational rationale: PANDORA degraded network-dependent F-22s/F-35s.
  A-10's mechanical simplicity = PANDORA resilience. Crodyn military mismanagement
  never retired them. Real-world retirement debates in game resolved — "they brought
  them back. All of them." [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

--- GAME 3 SPOOK — YUNNAN-SHANGHAI SEQUENCE SKETCH ---

Status: Early sketch. No confirmed structure.

Reason for China mission: Wei Junlong's Taiwanese semiconductor engineer is in Chinese
  custody post-Taiwan annexation. Engineer is Wei's vulnerability. Spook wants to
  use that leverage to either extract the engineer or compel Wei's cooperation.
  [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3]

La Avispa returns: Her Southeast Asian criminal network contacts make the Laos-Yunnan
  approach possible. Also: unfinished business with Spook. [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3]

Route: Laos → Yunnan province jungle crossing (compressed, not fully simulated) →
  overland through Yunnan (truck, boat, contact network) → Shanghai.

Cover: Nature photographers (credible for Yunnan biodiversity geography).

Jungle crossing key moments:
  1. Movement sequence establishing terrain difficulty (short, ~5 min gameplay).
  2. Near-miss patrol encounter — team goes completely still.
  3. Hillside pass reveal — valley view, karst mountains, helicopter scene.
  4. La Avispa border crossing moment — her skills visible, character moment with Spook.
  [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3 SKETCH]

Helicopter scene (Yunnan valley): Hillside pass, gap in trees. Green valley, river,
  karst mountains if geography supports. Orange/red sunset sky. Formation of PLA
  helicopters (Z-20s or Z-10s) crosses sky — receding toward objective, silhouette
  at distance. Sound: overlapping rotor throb. No music. Hostile helicopters double
  as orientation device — player can follow their flight path to understand where
  the objective is. [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3 SKETCH]

Shanghai endgame: Dense urban environment. Older districts — French Concession,
  Tianzifang area. Kane & Lynch 2 aesthetic — narrow lanes, low buildings, neon
  signage, cramped restaurant kitchens, tiled rooms, the Pudong skyline visible
  above. High surveillance density paradoxically makes disappearing easier for
  skilled operators. [PROVISIONAL — GAME 3 SKETCH]

--- GAME 3 DUCKY CAMPAIGN ---
Not yet developed. [FLAGGED — ENTIRELY UNMAPPED]

September 3rd, 2028: PANDORA attacks. US nationwide cyber attack. West Coast
  amphibious invasion begins. Russia opens Baltic front. China invades Taiwan.
  Spook confronts Goldberg on East McFarlane Island simultaneously.
  First reported: 1033 PST by local media. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

November 3rd, 2028: US Presidential Election (suspended by Crodyn via SCOTUS ruling
  under wartime emergency provisions). Exactly two months after PANDORA. [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

June 4th, 2028: Glushkin activation by Lebedev/Nasmith at Specter Aerospace, Peabody MA.
  91 days before PANDORA attacks. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

Lebedev activation: Approximately 3 months before PANDORA attacks (early June 2028).
  [CONFIRMED IN NOTES]

Game 2 Romeo campaign: Begins approximately Day 31 of Calloway occupation (early-to-mid
  October 2028). Presidential address falls late October or very early November 2028 —
  within days of the suspended election date. [SIDEBAR CONFIRMED]

PROJECT WARRIORS — CAMPAIGN TEASER TREATMENTS
Sidebar Promotional Development Thread — Master File v1.0
================================================================
NOTE TO OTHER THREADS: This file was developed in a dedicated
promotional/sidebar thread separate from the main narrative,
gameplay, and worldbuilding threads. All decisions here are
creative/promotional in nature and do not constitute canonical
story changes. Cross-reference with main narrative thread before
treating any specific detail as locked canon.
================================================================


OVERVIEW & WORKING METHOD
--------------------------
This file documents the full teaser video treatments for all three
Game 2 campaigns developed in the promotional sidebar thread, along
with the creative rationale, collaborative decisions, and principles
that emerged from the development process. It is intended to be
uploaded to the project knowledge base so that future threads can
benefit from what was established here.

The three teasers were developed sequentially — Romeo first, then
Ducky, then Spook — using a consistent method: Claude proposed a
full concept, Stefan responded with additions and modifications,
and each treatment was refined through that exchange before being
written up as a clean final document. All final creative calls
were made by Stefan.


CONFIRMED TAGLINES (FINAL, ALL THREE CAMPAIGNS)
-------------------------------------------------
AMERICAN FREEDOM:       "War Hits Home."
AEGIS FALLS:            "The System Fell. We Didn't."
GODKILLER:              "You Can't Kill A Dead Man."

NOTE ON TAGLINE DEVELOPMENT:
- "War Hits Home" was Stefan's original and was kept unchanged.
- "The System Fell. We Didn't." was proposed by Claude as a
  replacement for Stefan's original "We Are Taking Our Home Back."
  Stefan accepted it as stronger and more specific to the campaign's
  betrayal/institutional collapse architecture.
- "You Can't Kill A Dead Man." is a shortened version of Stefan's
  original "How Do You Kill A Man Who's Already Dead?" — the
  truncation was proposed by Claude for punch and pacing and
  confirmed by Stefan as a clear improvement.

CONFIRMED MUSIC (ALL THREE CAMPAIGNS)
--------------------------------------
AMERICAN FREEDOM:   "Good Morning America" — Jesse Welles
AEGIS FALLS:        "Kyiv" — Apashe ft. Alina Pash
GODKILLER:          "King Nothing" — Metallica

NOTE: All music selections carry commercial licensing flags.
Acknowledged as a future constraint, not a current creative blocker.

RELEASE DATE USED IN ALL THREE TEASERS: Coming Q2 2028
NOTE: This date is invented flavor only and does not reflect any
actual development or release timeline.


SHARED FORMAT SPECS (ALL THREE TEASERS)
-----------------------------------------
- Runtime: approx. 90 seconds each
- Aspect ratio: 2.39:1 cinematic widescreen
- No HUD, no gameplay footage
- No dialogue in Romeo or Ducky teasers
- Godkiller contains two lines of spoken dialogue at the close only
  (see Godkiller treatment below — this was a deliberate exception
  confirmed by Stefan)
- Title cards: plain white text, no fanfare, no music beneath them,
  one beat between each card


CAMPAIGN-BY-CAMPAIGN EMOTIONAL REGISTER SUMMARY
-------------------------------------------------
AMERICAN FREEDOM (Romeo):
  Elegiac, documentary, grief before defiance. The teaser shows
  what has been lost before it shows any resistance. Emotional
  architecture: grief → weight → quiet defiance → reckoning.

AEGIS FALLS (Ducky):
  Dread and institutional fracture. The feeling of standing on a
  fault line the moment before it gives. Emotional architecture:
  trust → creeping wrongness → operational chaos → the promise
  broken. The returning AEGIS emblem (pristine → cracked →
  fractured) is the visual spine.

GODKILLER (Spook):
  Psychological menace and the gap between official truth and
  actual truth. Investigative rather than action-driven. Emotional
  architecture: institutional certainty → evidence of deception →
  the hunt → the confrontation of two men who understand each other
  completely.


KEY CREATIVE DECISIONS MADE IN THIS THREAD
--------------------------------------------
1. CHORAL ARRANGEMENT — AMERICAN FREEDOM CLOSE
   Stefan's suggestion: the Good Morning America melody transitions
   in the final act not to a music swell but to a sparse unaccompanied
   mixed choir arrangement. Tonal reference: "Keep Your Rifle By Your
   Side" from the Ken Burns Civil War soundtrack — voices that sound
   like they belong to the land, somewhere between a hymn and a lament.
   The effect: Romeo at the tree line stops being one soldier and
   becomes something larger. The melody now belongs to everyone in
   the town. Hard cut to black stops the choir mid-phrase — the
   silence lands harder for what it interrupted.

2. THREE-FRAME CODY BEAUMONT IMAGE — AMERICAN FREEDOM BUILD SECTION
   Stefan's suggestion: buried in the quick cuts of Act Three, lasting
   approximately three frames (roughly one eighth of a second at 24fps),
   is a flash of the Cody Beaumont death image — the ambiguous loading
   screen photograph that is one of the campaign's most emotionally
   loaded visual assets. It is not acknowledged by the edit around it.
   It is gone before the conscious mind fully forms the question.
   Placement confirmed: inside the momentum of the build section cuts,
   not near the emotional close. Purpose: plants subconscious unease,
   rewards frame-by-frame analysis, respects the intelligence of the
   audience, generates organic discovery/discussion post-release.
   Both Stefan and Claude independently arrived at the same placement
   instinct — confirmed as correct.

3. RAW POV/DRONE FOOTAGE GRAMMAR — AEGIS FALLS
   Stefan's suggestion: some of the quick cuts in Ducky's teaser
   should reference the visual grammar of modern warfare as audiences
   now know it from Ukrainian war footage online — GoPro helmet
   footage, drone POV, night vision green, thermal white-hot
   signatures, handheld phone video with blown-out audio. The
   frequency of this raw footage material should ramp up and down
   in sync with the music and pacing — rare during the measured
   opening acts, bleeding in with increasing frequency during the
   build, peaking near the climax, then receding as the music
   hollows out toward the close. First act kept entirely cinematic
   so the raw footage's first appearance carries weight as an
   intrusion. Claude confirmed this is not a step in the wrong
   direction — it has real cinematic and editorial precedent and
   the ramp logic is sophisticated and correct.

4. TWO LINES OF DIALOGUE — GODKILLER CLOSE
   The only spoken words across all three teasers appear at the
   close of Godkiller:
     SPOOK: "You can't kill a dead man."
     GOLDBERG (O.S.): "No."
   Rationale: the tagline IS dialogue, and hearing it spoken lands
   differently than reading it. Goldberg's single-word response —
   calm, faintly amused — is more unsettling than any image.
   It establishes his presence without showing his face clearly.
   Stefan confirmed: keep the dialogue. Do not apply the no-dialogue
   rule to Godkiller.

5. RETURNING EMBLEM STRUCTURE — AEGIS FALLS
   The AEGIS emblem appears three times across the teaser —
   Act One (pristine), Act Two close (hairline crack, easy to miss),
   Act Four (spider web fracture, still holding its shape, still
   recognizable, motto still legible). The visual argument made
   without words: the system you trusted was already cracking.
   You just couldn't see it yet.

6. EAST MCFARLANE ISLAND — GODKILLER
   Appears in Act Three as the cut that sits longer than everything
   around it — wide aerial, golden hour, Goldberg alive and unhurried
   on a terrace overlooking the water. His posture is that of a man
   who has decided he is entirely beyond reach. This image is load-
   bearing: it confirms to the audience that the DECEASED stamp was
   wrong, without a single word of explanation.


NOTES FOR FUTURE DEVELOPMENT IN THIS THREAD
---------------------------------------------
The following items were flagged during teaser development as
next steps for this promotional sidebar thread:

1. KEY ART — one hero image per campaign. The single image that
   goes on a billboard, a Steam page, a magazine spread. Locks
   in the visual identity of each campaign. To be developed next.

2. SECONDARY FORMATS — loading screen teasers, social media drip
   content, print ads, possibly diegetic in-universe artifacts
   (newspaper front pages, redacted documents, ARG-style website
   content). To follow key art.

3. AEGIS FALLS TEASER — PLACEHOLDER NOTE
   The AEGIS Falls teaser currently uses first-game locations and
   operational geography as placeholder scaffolding, since Ducky's
   Game 2 campaign (Persistent Threat) has not yet been fully
   developed in the main narrative thread. Stefan confirmed this
   is acceptable at this stage of development. Flag for revisit
   when the main thread catches up with Persistent Threat mission
   development.

4. CHARACTER PROMO CLIP SERIES — flagged in main thread, to be
   developed in the music/audio thread. Starting with Switchblade.
   60-90 seconds, tone varies by character. Not yet started in
   this sidebar thread.
